PREFACE
   This code of the City of Clatskanie, as supplemented, contains ordinances up
to and including ordinance 707, passed June 7, 2023. Ordinances of the City
adopted after said ordinance supersede the provisions of this code to the
extent that they are in conflict or inconsistent therewith. Consult the City
office in order to ascertain whether any particular provision of the code has
been amended, superseded or repealed.
American Legal Publishing
Cincinnati, Ohio
ORDINANCES PENDING CODIFICATION
Listed ordinances have been passed, but they have not been incorporated into
the code and they may not show the original ordinances in their entirety.
Please contact the office of the clerk if there are any questions concerning
the ordinances listed.
ADOPTING ORDINANCE
ORDINANCE NO. 644
   REVISING, CODIFYING AND COMPILING THE GENERAL ORDINANCES
   OF THE CITY OF CLATSKANIE, OREGON, AND
   ADOPTING THE CLATSKANIE CITY CODE
Whereas, the city council seeks to update and modernize the Clatskanie city
code in order to establish more efficient and effective city governance; and
Whereas, the Clatskanie planning commission and the city council have held
multiple meetings and public hearings over the course of several months to
discuss proposed changes to the code and solicit public input; and
Whereas, Sterling Codifiers, Inc. is a qualified codification service and has
produced the city code in an updated and digitized format.
NOW THEREFORE THE CITY OF CLATSKANIE ORDAINS AS FOLLOWS:
   Section 1: Pursuant to the provisions of ORS 221.310 et seq., and from and
after the date of passage of this ordinance, the city code of the city of
Clatskanie, Oregon prepared by Sterling Codifiers, Inc. containing the
compilation of all ordinances of a general nature together with the changes
made to said ordinances through ordinance no. 631 adopted on March 3, 2004,
under the direction of the governing body of the city, shall be accepted in all
courts without question as the official code and law of the city as enacted by
the mayor and city council.
   Section 2: There is hereby adopted, as a method of perpetual codification,
the loose-leaf type of binding together with the continuous supplement service,
provided by a codification service approved by the city, whereby each newly
adopted ordinance of a general and permanent nature amending, altering, adding
or deleting provisions of the official city code is identified by the proper
catchline and is inserted in the proper place in each of the official copies,
one copy of which shall be maintained in the office of the city manager,
certified as to correctness and available for inspection at any and all times
that said office is regularly open.
   Section 3: All ordinances of a general nature included in this official city
code shall be considered as a continuation of said ordinance provision and the
fact that some provisions have been deliberately eliminated by the governing
body shall not serve to cause any interruption in the continuous effectiveness
of ordinances included in said official city code. All ordinances of a special
nature, such as tax levy ordinances, bond ordinances, franchises, vacating
ordinances and annexation ordinances shall continue in full force and effect
unless specifically repealed or amended by a provision of the city code. Such
ordinances are not intended to be included in the official city code.
   Section 4: It shall be unlawful for any person, firm or corporation to
change or amend by additions or deletions, any part or portion of such code, or
to insert or delete pages or portions thereof, or to alter or tamper with such
code in any manner whatsoever which will cause the law of the city to be
misrepresented thereby.
   Section 5: Any violation of any provision of this ordinance hereby adopted
shall be punishable by a fine not to exceed one hundred dollars ($100.00) per
occurrence.
   Section 6: All ordinances or parts of ordinances in conflict herewith, are,
to the extent of such conflict, hereby repealed.
   Section 7: Sterling Codifiers, Inc, has prepared and made available in
digital form the Clatskanie city code at the website: www.sterlingcodifiers.com
and amendments hereto attached as exhibit "A" to this ordinance are hereby
adopted.
   Section 8: This ordinance and the code adopted by the same shall be
effective thirty days after passage on the date listed below.
Passed by the council of the city of Clatskanie this 1st day of March 2006.
            Diane Pohl, Mayor
Attest:         
   Tina Hendricks, CMC
   City Recorder
1st Reading:   February 15, 2006
2nd Reading:   March 1, 2006
